
event `Senza Solaria Stocks Aluminum`
	outfitter "Senza Solaria Plugin Outfits"
		`Aluminum`
mission `Senza Solaria Supply Aluminum`
	invisible
	landing
	source
		planet "Senza Solaria"
	to offer
		has `outfit (cargo): Aluminum`
	on offer
		conversation
			scene "outfit/harvested aluminum"
			`Upon arriving at Senza Solaria, before you can even decide where to go, a group of researchers are already there to meet you the moment you step off of your ship.`
			`	"Our scanners detected an unknown outfit aboard your ship, would you be willing to donate it for us to reverse engineer?" says a researcher.`
			choice
				`	(Donate the Aluminum to be researched.)`
					goto donate
				`	(Don't donate.)`
					defer
			label donate
			`"Ah, perfect! We appreciate your donation, and assure you, your contribution will not go to waste!"`
			`The engineers carefully extract the donation from your ship, and take it to their research facility to reverse engineer."`
			``
			`	After idling at the spaceport for a few hours, you hear rumors of a new stock arriving soon at Senza Solaria.`
				accept
	on accept
		outfit `Aluminum` -1
		event `Senza Solaria Stocks Aluminum`


event `Senza Solaria Stocks Copper`
	outfitter "Senza Solaria Plugin Outfits"
		`Copper`
mission `Senza Solaria Supply Copper`
	invisible
	landing
	source

	to offer
		has `outfit (cargo): Copper`
	on offer
		conversation
			scene "outfit/harvested copper"
			`Upon arriving at Senza Solaria, before you can even decide where to go, a group of researchers are already there to meet you the moment you step off of your ship.`
			`	"Our scanners detected an unknown outfit aboard your ship, would you be willing to donate it for us to reverse engineer?" says a researcher.`
			choice
				`	(Donate the Copper to be researched.)`
					goto donate
				`	(Don't donate.)`
					defer
			label donate
			`"Ah, perfect! We appreciate your donation, and assure you, your contribution will not go to waste!"`
			`The engineers carefully extract the donation from your ship, and take it to their research facility to reverse engineer."`
			``
			`	After idling at the spaceport for a few hours, you hear rumors of a new stock arriving soon at Senza Solaria.`
				accept
	on accept
		outfit `Copper` -1
		event `Senza Solaria Stocks Copper`

				`	(Donate the Quarg Skylance to be researched.)`
					goto donate
				`	(Don't donate.)`
					defer
			label donate
			`"Ah, perfect! We appreciate your donation, and assure you, your contribution will not go to waste!"`
			`The engineers carefully extract the donation from your ship, and take it to their research facility to reverse engineer."`
			``
			`	After idling at the spaceport for a few hours, you hear rumors of a new stock arriving soon at Senza Solaria.`
				accept
	on accept
		outfit `Quarg Skylance` -1
		event `Senza Solaria Stocks Quarg Skylance`
